href=\"https://www.lambdatest.com/playwright\" h=\"ID=SERP,5521.1\" target=\"_blank\"><div class=\"df_alsoAskCard rqnaAnsCWrapper df_vt\" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.Item\" data-query=\"What is playwright API?\" data-iid=\"SERP.5518\" data-parentiid=\"SERP.5519\"><div class=\"df_qnacontent\"><div class=\"df_qntextwithicn\"><div class=\"df_qntext\">What is playwright API?</div></div><span class=\"df_alsocon b_primtxt HitHighlightWrapper \" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.ItemDetails\">Built by Microsoft, Playwright is a <strong>Node.js library</strong> that, with a single API, automates websites and web apps running on Chromium, Firefox, and WebKit. These APIs can be used by developers writing JavaScript code to create new browser pages, navigate to URLs, and then interact with elements on a page.</span></div><div class=\"df_ansatb df_ansfontlghybrid\"><div class=\"qna_algo df_qna_algo\"><div class=\"b_algo\"><h2><span class=\"\">What Is Playwright: A Tutorial on How to Use Playwright</span></h2></div><div class=\"b_attribution b_clearfix qfavc\"><div class=\"b_imagePair\"><div class=\"cico\" style=\"width:16px;height:16px;\"><img src=\"https://th.bing.com/th/id/ODLS.301ea3e3-90b4-45b0-bb9a-c5ec31733a59?w=16&amp;h=16&amp;c=7&amp;r=0&amp;o=6&amp;pid=1.7\" height=\"16\" width=\"16\" role=\"presentation\" class=\"rms_img\" data-bm=\"43\"></div><div><div class=\"qna_attr\"><cite>lambdatest.com</cite></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></a></div><div class=\"slide\" data-dataurl=\"\" data-rinterval=\"\" data-appns=\"SERP\" data-k=\"5649.1\" data-tag=\"\" style=\"\" tabindex=\"0\" data-mini=\"\" role=\"listitem\"><a class=\"df_alsocon_link\" aria-label=\"https://playwright.dev/docs/intro\" href=\"https://playwright.dev/docs/intro\" h=\"ID=SERP,5526.1\" target=\"_blank\"><div class=\"df_alsoAskCard rqnaAnsCWrapper df_vt\" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.Item\" data-query=\"What is playwright test?\" data-iid=\"SERP.5523\" data-parentiid=\"SERP.5524\"><div class=\"df_qnacontent\"><div class=\"df_qntextwithicn\"><div class=\"df_qntext\">What is playwright test?</div></div><span class=\"df_alsocon b_primtxt HitHighlightWrapper \" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.ItemDetails\">Playwright Test was created specifically to accommodate the needs of <strong>end-to-end testing</strong>. Playwright supports all modern rendering engines including Chromium, WebKit, and Firefox. Test on Windows, Linux, and macOS, locally or on CI, headless or headed with native mobile emulation of Google Chrome for Android and Mobile Safari. You will learn</span></div><div class=\"df_ansatb df_ansfontlghybrid\"><div class=\"qna_algo df_qna_algo\"><div class=\"b_algo\"><h2><span class=\"\">Installation | Playwright</span></h2></div><div class=\"b_attribution b_clearfix qfavc\"><div class=\"b_imagePair\"><div class=\"cico\" style=\"width:16px;height:16px;\"><img src=\"https://th.bing.com/th/id/ODLS.A2450BEC-5595-40BA-9F13-D9EC6AB74B9F?w=16&amp;h=16&amp;c=7&amp;r=0&amp;o=6&amp;pid=1.7\" height=\"16\" width=\"16\" role=\"presentation\" class=\"rms_img\" data-bm=\"44\"></div><div><div class=\"qna_attr\"><cite>playwright.dev</cite></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></a></div><div class=\"slide\" data-dataurl=\"\" data-rinterval=\"\" data-appns=\"SERP\" data-k=\"5650.1\" data-tag=\"\" style=\"\" tabindex=\"0\" data-mini=\"\" role=\"listitem\"><a class=\"df_alsocon_link\" aria-label=\"https://github.com/microsoft/playwright\" href=\"https://github.com/microsoft/playwright\" h=\"ID=SERP,5531.1\" target=\"_blank\"><div class=\"df_alsoAskCard rqnaAnsCWrapper df_vt\" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.Item\" data-query=\"What is playwright framework?\" data-iid=\"SERP.5528\" data-parentiid=\"SERP.5529\"><div class=\"df_qnacontent\"><div class=\"df_qntextwithicn\"><div class=\"df_qntext\">What is playwright framework?</div></div><span class=\"df_alsocon b_primtxt HitHighlightWrapper \" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.ItemDetails\">Playwright is a <strong>framework for Web Testing and Automation</strong>. It allows testing Chromium, Firefox and WebKit with a single API. Playwright is built to enable cross-browser web automation that is ever-green, capable, reliable and fast. Headless execution is supported for all browsers on all platforms. Check out system requirements for details.</span></div><div class=\"df_ansatb df_ansfontlghybrid\"><div class=\"qna_algo df_qna_algo\"><div class=\"b_algo\"><h2><span class=\"\">Playwright - GitHub</span></h2></div><div class=\"b_attribution b_clearfix qfavc\"><div class=\"b_imagePair\"><div class=\"cico\" style=\"width:16px;height:16px;\"><img src=\"https://th.bing.com/th/id/ODLS.b2099a11-ca12-45ce-bede-5df940e38a48?w=16&amp;h=16&amp;c=7&amp;r=0&amp;o=6&amp;pid=1.7\" height=\"16\" width=\"16\" role=\"presentation\" class=\"rms_img\" data-bm=\"45\"></div><div><div class=\"qna_attr\"><cite>github.com</cite></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></a></div><div class=\"slide\" data-dataurl=\"\" data-rinterval=\"\" data-appns=\"SERP\" data-k=\"5651.1\" data-tag=\"\" style=\"\" tabindex=\"0\" data-mini=\"\" role=\"listitem\"><a class=\"df_alsocon_link\" aria-label=\"https://playwright.dev/\" href=\"https://playwright.dev/\" h=\"ID=SERP,5536.1\" target=\"_blank\"><div class=\"df_alsoAskCard rqnaAnsCWrapper df_vt\" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.Item\" data-query=\"What is a playwright assertion?\" data-iid=\"SERP.5533\" data-parentiid=\"SERP.5534\"><div class=\"df_qnacontent\"><div class=\"df_qntextwithicn\"><div class=\"df_qntext\">What is a playwright assertion?</div></div><span class=\"df_alsocon b_primtxt HitHighlightWrapper \" data-tag=\"RelatedQnA.ItemDetails\">Auto-wait. Playwright waits for elements to be actionable prior to performing actions. It also has a rich set of introspection events. The combination of the two eliminates the need for artificial timeouts - the primary cause of flaky tests. Web-first assertions. Playwright assertions are <strong>created specifically for the dynamic web</strong>.</span></div><div class=\"df_ansatb df_ansfontlghybrid\"><div class=\"qna_algo df_qna_algo\"><div
